4508      * @param target the method handle to invoke after arguments are reordered
4509      * @param newType the expected type of the new method handle
4510      * @param reorder an index array which controls the reordering
4511      * @return a method handle which delegates to the target after it
4512      *           drops unused arguments and moves and/or duplicates the other arguments
4513      * @throws NullPointerException if any argument is null
4514      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if the index array length is not equal to
4515      *                  the arity of the target, or if any index array element
4516      *                  not a valid index for a parameter of {@code newType},
4517      *                  or if two corresponding parameter types in
4518      *                  {@code target.type()} and {@code newType} are not identical,
4519      */
4520     public static MethodHandle permuteArguments(MethodHandle target, MethodType newType, int... reorder) {
4521         reorder = reorder.clone();  // get a private copy
4522         MethodType oldType = target.type();
4523         permuteArgumentChecks(reorder, newType, oldType);
4524         // first detect dropped arguments and handle them separately
4525         int[] originalReorder = reorder;
4526         BoundMethodHandle result = target.rebind();
4527         LambdaForm form = result.form;
4528         int newArity = newType.parameterCount();
4529         // Normalize the reordering into a real permutation,
4530         // by removing duplicates and adding dropped elements.
4531         // This somewhat improves lambda form caching, as well
4532         // as simplifying the transform by breaking it up into steps.
4533         for (int ddIdx; (ddIdx = findFirstDupOrDrop(reorder, newArity)) != 0; ) {
4534             if (ddIdx > 0) {
4535                 // We found a duplicated entry at reorder[ddIdx].
4536                 // Example:  (x,y,z)->asList(x,y,z)
4537                 // permuted by [1*,0,1] => (a0,a1)=>asList(a1,a0,a1)
4538                 // permuted by [0,1,0*] => (a0,a1)=>asList(a0,a1,a0)
4539                 // The starred element corresponds to the argument
4540                 // deleted by the dupArgumentForm transform.
4541                 int srcPos = ddIdx, dstPos = srcPos, dupVal = reorder[srcPos];
4542                 boolean killFirst = false;
4543                 for (int val; (val = reorder[--dstPos]) != dupVal; ) {
4544                     // Set killFirst if the dup is larger than an intervening position.
4545                     // This will remove at least one inversion from the permutation.
4546                     if (dupVal > val) killFirst = true;
4547                 }
4548                 if (!killFirst) {
4549                     srcPos = dstPos;
4550                     dstPos = ddIdx;
4551                 }
4552                 form = form.editor().dupArgumentForm(1 + srcPos, 1 + dstPos);
4553                 assert (reorder[srcPos] == reorder[dstPos]);
4554                 oldType = oldType.dropParameterTypes(dstPos, dstPos + 1);
4555                 // contract the reordering by removing the element at dstPos
4556                 int tailPos = dstPos + 1;
4557                 System.arraycopy(reorder, tailPos, reorder, dstPos, reorder.length - tailPos);
4558                 reorder = Arrays.copyOf(reorder, reorder.length - 1);
4559             } else {
4560                 int dropVal = ~ddIdx, insPos = 0;
4561                 while (insPos < reorder.length && reorder[insPos] < dropVal) {
4562                     // Find first element of reorder larger than dropVal.
4563                     // This is where we will insert the dropVal.
4564                     insPos += 1;
4565                 }
4566                 Class<?> ptype = newType.parameterType(dropVal);
4567                 form = form.editor().addArgumentForm(1 + insPos, BasicType.basicType(ptype));
4568                 oldType = oldType.insertParameterTypes(insPos, ptype);
4569                 // expand the reordering by inserting an element at insPos
4570                 int tailPos = insPos + 1;
4571                 reorder = Arrays.copyOf(reorder, reorder.length + 1);
4572                 System.arraycopy(reorder, insPos, reorder, tailPos, reorder.length - tailPos);
4573                 reorder[insPos] = dropVal;
4574             }
4575             assert (permuteArgumentChecks(reorder, newType, oldType));
4576         }
4577         assert (reorder.length == newArity);  // a perfect permutation
4578         // Note:  This may cache too many distinct LFs. Consider backing off to varargs code.
4579         form = form.editor().permuteArgumentsForm(1, reorder);
4580         if (newType == result.type() && form == result.internalForm())
4581             return result;
4582         return result.copyWith(newType, form);
4583     }
4584 
4585     /**
4586      * Return an indication of any duplicate or omission in reorder.
4587      * If the reorder contains a duplicate entry, return the index of the second occurrence.
4588      * Otherwise, return ~(n), for the first n in [0..newArity-1] that is not present in reorder.
4589      * Otherwise, return zero.
4590      * If an element not in [0..newArity-1] is encountered, return reorder.length.
4591      */
4592     private static int findFirstDupOrDrop(int[] reorder, int newArity) {
4593         final int BIT_LIMIT = 63;  // max number of bits in bit mask
4594         if (newArity < BIT_LIMIT) {
4595             long mask = 0;
4596             for (int i = 0; i < reorder.length; i++) {
4597                 int arg = reorder[i];
4598                 if (arg >= newArity) {
4599                     return reorder.length;
4600                 }
4601                 long bit = 1L << arg;
4602                 if ((mask & bit) != 0) {
4603                     return i;  // >0 indicates a dup
4604                 }
4605                 mask |= bit;
4606             }
4607             if (mask == (1L << newArity) - 1) {
4608                 assert(Long.numberOfTrailingZeros(Long.lowestOneBit(~mask)) == newArity);
4609                 return 0;
4610             }
4611             // find first zero
4612             long zeroBit = Long.lowestOneBit(~mask);
4613             int zeroPos = Long.numberOfTrailingZeros(zeroBit);
4614             assert(zeroPos <= newArity);
4615             if (zeroPos == newArity) {
4616                 return 0;
4617             }
4618             return ~zeroPos;
4619         } else {
4620             // same algorithm, different bit set
4621             BitSet mask = new BitSet(newArity);
4622             for (int i = 0; i < reorder.length; i++) {
4623                 int arg = reorder[i];
4624                 if (arg >= newArity) {
4625                     return reorder.length;
4626                 }
4627                 if (mask.get(arg)) {
4628                     return i;  // >0 indicates a dup
4629                 }
4630                 mask.set(arg);
4631             }
4632             int zeroPos = mask.nextClearBit(0);
4633             assert(zeroPos <= newArity);
4634             if (zeroPos == newArity) {
4635                 return 0;
4636             }
4637             return ~zeroPos;
4638         }
4639     }
4640 
4641     static boolean permuteArgumentChecks(int[] reorder, MethodType newType, MethodType oldType) {
4642         if (newType.returnType() != oldType.returnType())
4643             throw newIllegalArgumentException("return types do not match",
4644                     oldType, newType);
4645         if (reorder.length == oldType.parameterCount()) {
4646             int limit = newType.parameterCount();
4647             boolean bad = false;
4648             for (int j = 0; j < reorder.length; j++) {
4649                 int i = reorder[j];
4650                 if (i < 0 || i >= limit) {
4651                     bad = true; break;
4652                 }
4653                 Class<?> src = newType.parameterType(i);
4654                 Class<?> dst = oldType.parameterType(j);
4655                 if (src != dst)
4656                     throw newIllegalArgumentException("parameter types do not match after reorder",
4657                             oldType, newType);
4658             }
4659             if (!bad)  return true;
4660         }
4661         throw newIllegalArgumentException("bad reorder array: "+Arrays.toString(reorder));
4662     }
4663 
4664     /**
4665      * Produces a method handle of the requested return type which returns the given
4666      * constant value every time it is invoked.
4667      * <p>
4668      * Before the method handle is returned, the passed-in value is converted to the requested type.
4669      * If the requested type is primitive, widening primitive conversions are attempted,
4670      * else reference conversions are attempted.
4671      * <p>The returned method handle is equivalent to {@code identity(type).bindTo(value)}.
4672      * @param type the return type of the desired method handle
4673      * @param value the value to return
4674      * @return a method handle of the given return type and no arguments, which always returns the given value
4675      * @throws NullPointerException if the {@code type} argument is null
4676      * @throws ClassCastException if the value cannot be converted to the required return type
4677      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if the given type is {@code void.class}
4678      */
4679     public static MethodHandle constant(Class<?> type, Object value) {
4680         if (type.isPrimitive()) {
4681             if (type == void.class)
4682                 throw newIllegalArgumentException("void type");
4683             Wrapper w = Wrapper.forPrimitiveType(type);
4684             value = w.convert(value, type);
4685             if (w.zero().equals(value))
4686                 return zero(w, type);
4687             return insertArguments(identity(type), 0, value);
4688         } else {
4689             if (value == null)
4690                 return zero(Wrapper.OBJECT, type);
4691             return identity(type).bindTo(value);
4692         }
4693     }
4694 
4695     /**
4696      * Produces a method handle which returns its sole argument when invoked.
4697      * @param type the type of the sole parameter and return value of the desired method handle
4698      * @return a unary method handle which accepts and returns the given type
4699      * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is null
4700      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if the given type is {@code void.class}
4701      */
4702     public static MethodHandle identity(Class<?> type) {
4703         Wrapper btw = (type.isPrimitive() ? Wrapper.forPrimitiveType(type) : Wrapper.OBJECT);
4704         int pos = btw.ordinal();
4705         MethodHandle ident = IDENTITY_MHS[pos];
4706         if (ident == null) {
4707             ident = setCachedMethodHandle(IDENTITY_MHS, pos, makeIdentity(btw.primitiveType()));
4708         }
4709         if (ident.type().returnType() == type)
4710             return ident;
4711         // something like identity(Foo.class); do not bother to intern these
4712         assert (btw == Wrapper.OBJECT);
4713         return makeIdentity(type);
4714     }
4715 
4716     /**
4717      * Produces a constant method handle of the requested return type which
4718      * returns the default value for that type every time it is invoked.
4719      * The resulting constant method handle will have no side effects.
4720      * <p>The returned method handle is equivalent to {@code empty(methodType(type))}.
4721      * It is also equivalent to {@code explicitCastArguments(constant(Object.class, null), methodType(type))},
4722      * since {@code explicitCastArguments} converts {@code null} to default values.
4723      * @param type the expected return type of the desired method handle
4724      * @return a constant method handle that takes no arguments
4725      *         and returns the default value of the given type (or void, if the type is void)
4726      * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is null
4727      * @see MethodHandles#constant
4728      * @see MethodHandles#empty
4729      * @see MethodHandles#explicitCastArguments
4730      * @since 9
4731      */
4732     public static MethodHandle zero(Class<?> type) {
4733         Objects.requireNonNull(type);
4734         if (type.isPrimitive()) {
4735             return zero(Wrapper.forPrimitiveType(type), type);
4736         } else if (type.isInlineClass()) {
4737             throw new UnsupportedOperationException();
4738         } else {
4739             return zero(Wrapper.OBJECT, type);
4740         }
4741     }
4742 
4743     private static MethodHandle identityOrVoid(Class<?> type) {
4744         return type == void.class ? zero(type) : identity(type);
4745     }
4746 
4747     /**
4748      * Produces a method handle of the requested type which ignores any arguments, does nothing,
4749      * and returns a suitable default depending on the return type.
4750      * That is, it returns a zero primitive value, a {@code null}, or {@code void}.
4751      * <p>The returned method handle is equivalent to
4752      * {@code dropArguments(zero(type.returnType()), 0, type.parameterList())}.
4753      *
4754      * @apiNote Given a predicate and target, a useful "if-then" construct can be produced as
4755      * {@code guardWithTest(pred, target, empty(target.type())}.
4756      * @param type the type of the desired method handle
4757      * @return a constant method handle of the given type, which returns a default value of the given return type
4758      * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is null
4759      * @see MethodHandles#zero
4760      * @see MethodHandles#constant
4761      * @since 9
4762      */
4763     public static  MethodHandle empty(MethodType type) {
4764         Objects.requireNonNull(type);
4765         return dropArguments(zero(type.returnType()), 0, type.parameterList());
4766     }
4767 
4768     private static final MethodHandle[] IDENTITY_MHS = new MethodHandle[Wrapper.COUNT];
4769     private static MethodHandle makeIdentity(Class<?> ptype) {
4770         MethodType mtype = MethodType.methodType(ptype, ptype);
4771         LambdaForm lform = LambdaForm.identityForm(BasicType.basicType(ptype));
4772         return MethodHandleImpl.makeIntrinsic(mtype, lform, Intrinsic.IDENTITY);
4773     }
4774 
4775     private static MethodHandle zero(Wrapper btw, Class<?> rtype) {
4776         int pos = btw.ordinal();
4777         MethodHandle zero = ZERO_MHS[pos];
4778         if (zero == null) {
4779             zero = setCachedMethodHandle(ZERO_MHS, pos, makeZero(btw.primitiveType()));
4780         }
4781         if (zero.type().returnType() == rtype)
4782             return zero;
4783         assert(btw == Wrapper.OBJECT);
4784         return makeZero(rtype);
4785     }
4786     private static final MethodHandle[] ZERO_MHS = new MethodHandle[Wrapper.COUNT];
4787     private static MethodHandle makeZero(Class<?> rtype) {
4788         MethodType mtype = methodType(rtype);
4789         LambdaForm lform = LambdaForm.zeroForm(BasicType.basicType(rtype));
4790         return MethodHandleImpl.makeIntrinsic(mtype, lform, Intrinsic.ZERO);
4791     }
4792 
4793     private static synchronized MethodHandle setCachedMethodHandle(MethodHandle[] cache, int pos, MethodHandle value) {
4794         // Simulate a CAS, to avoid racy duplication of results.
4795         MethodHandle prev = cache[pos];
4796         if (prev != null) return prev;
4797         return cache[pos] = value;
4798     }
4799 
4800     /**
4801      * Provides a target method handle with one or more <em>bound arguments</em>
4802      * in advance of the method handle's invocation.
4803      * The formal parameters to the target corresponding to the bound
4804      * arguments are called <em>bound parameters</em>.
4805      * Returns a new method handle which saves away the bound arguments.
4806      * When it is invoked, it receives arguments for any non-bound parameters,
4807      * binds the saved arguments to their corresponding parameters,
4808      * and calls the original target.
4809      * <p>
4810      * The type of the new method handle will drop the types for the bound
4811      * parameters from the original target type, since the new method handle
4812      * will no longer require those arguments to be supplied by its callers.
4813      * <p>
4814      * Each given argument object must match the corresponding bound parameter type.
4815      * If a bound parameter type is a primitive, the argument object
4816      * must be a wrapper, and will be unboxed to produce the primitive value.
4817      * <p>
4818      * The {@code pos} argument selects which parameters are to be bound.
4819      * It may range between zero and <i>N-L</i> (inclusively),
4820      * where <i>N</i> is the arity of the target method handle
4821      * and <i>L</i> is the length of the values array.
4822      * <p>
4823      * <em>Note:</em> The resulting adapter is never a {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector
4824      * variable-arity method handle}, even if the original target method handle was.
4825      * @param target the method handle to invoke after the argument is inserted
4826      * @param pos where to insert the argument (zero for the first)
4827      * @param values the series of arguments to insert
4828      * @return a method handle which inserts an additional argument,
4829      *         before calling the original method handle
4830      * @throws NullPointerException if the target or the {@code values} array is null
4831      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if (@code pos) is less than {@code 0} or greater than
4832      *         {@code N - L} where {@code N} is the arity of the target method handle and {@code L}
4833      *         is the length of the values array.
4834      * @throws ClassCastException if an argument does not match the corresponding bound parameter
4835      *         type.
4836      * @see MethodHandle#bindTo
4837      */
4838     public static MethodHandle insertArguments(MethodHandle target, int pos, Object... values) {
4839         int insCount = values.length;
4840         Class<?>[] ptypes = insertArgumentsChecks(target, insCount, pos);
4841         if (insCount == 0)  return target;
4842         BoundMethodHandle result = target.rebind();
4843         for (int i = 0; i < insCount; i++) {
4844             Object value = values[i];
4845             Class<?> ptype = ptypes[pos+i];
4846             if (ptype.isPrimitive()) {
4847                 result = insertArgumentPrimitive(result, pos, ptype, value);
4848             } else {
4849                 value = ptype.cast(value);  // throw CCE if needed
4850                 result = result.bindArgumentL(pos, value);
4851             }
4852         }
4853         return result;
4854     }
4855 
4856     private static BoundMethodHandle insertArgumentPrimitive(BoundMethodHandle result, int pos,
4857                                                              Class<?> ptype, Object value) {
4858         Wrapper w = Wrapper.forPrimitiveType(ptype);
4859         // perform unboxing and/or primitive conversion
4860         value = w.convert(value, ptype);
4861         switch (w) {
4862         case INT:     return result.bindArgumentI(pos, (int)value);
4863         case LONG:    return result.bindArgumentJ(pos, (long)value);
4864         case FLOAT:   return result.bindArgumentF(pos, (float)value);
4865         case DOUBLE:  return result.bindArgumentD(pos, (double)value);
4866         default:      return result.bindArgumentI(pos, ValueConversions.widenSubword(value));
4867         }
4868     }
4869 
4870     private static Class<?>[] insertArgumentsChecks(MethodHandle target, int insCount, int pos) throws RuntimeException {
4871         MethodType oldType = target.type();
4872         int outargs = oldType.parameterCount();
4873         int inargs  = outargs - insCount;
4874         if (inargs < 0)
4875             throw newIllegalArgumentException("too many values to insert");
4876         if (pos < 0 || pos > inargs)
4877             throw newIllegalArgumentException("no argument type to append");
4878         return oldType.ptypes();
4879     }
4880 
4881     /**
4882      * Produces a method handle which will discard some dummy arguments
4883      * before calling some other specified <i>target</i> method handle.
4884      * The type of the new method handle will be the same as the target's type,
4885      * except it will also include the dummy argument types,
4886      * at some given position.
4887      * <p>
4888      * The {@code pos} argument may range between zero and <i>N</i>,
4889      * where <i>N</i> is the arity of the target.
4890      * If {@code pos} is zero, the dummy arguments will precede
4891      * the target's real arguments; if {@code pos} is <i>N</i>
4892      * they will come after.
4893      * <p>
4894      * <b>Example:</b>
4895      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
4896 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodHandles.*;
4897 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodType.*;
4898 ...
4899 MethodHandle cat = lookup().findVirtual(String.class,
4900   "concat", methodType(String.class, String.class));
4901 assertEquals("xy", (String) cat.invokeExact("x", "y"));
4902 MethodType bigType = cat.type().insertParameterTypes(0, int.class, String.class);
4903 MethodHandle d0 = dropArguments(cat, 0, bigType.parameterList().subList(0,2));
4904 assertEquals(bigType, d0.type());
4905 assertEquals("yz", (String) d0.invokeExact(123, "x", "y", "z"));
4906      * }</pre></blockquote>
4907      * <p>
4908      * This method is also equivalent to the following code:
4909      * <blockquote><pre>
4910      * {@link #dropArguments(MethodHandle,int,Class...) dropArguments}{@code (target, pos, valueTypes.toArray(new Class[0]))}
4911      * </pre></blockquote>
4912      * @param target the method handle to invoke after the arguments are dropped
4913      * @param pos position of first argument to drop (zero for the leftmost)
4914      * @param valueTypes the type(s) of the argument(s) to drop
4915      * @return a method handle which drops arguments of the given types,
4916      *         before calling the original method handle
4917      * @throws NullPointerException if the target is null,
4918      *                              or if the {@code valueTypes} list or any of its elements is null
4919      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if any element of {@code valueTypes} is {@code void.class},
4920      *                  or if {@code pos} is negative or greater than the arity of the target,
4921      *                  or if the new method handle's type would have too many parameters
4922      */
4923     public static MethodHandle dropArguments(MethodHandle target, int pos, List<Class<?>> valueTypes) {
4924         return dropArguments0(target, pos, copyTypes(valueTypes.toArray()));
4925     }
4926 
4927     private static List<Class<?>> copyTypes(Object[] array) {
4928         return Arrays.asList(Arrays.copyOf(array, array.length, Class[].class));
4929     }
4930 
4931     private static MethodHandle dropArguments0(MethodHandle target, int pos, List<Class<?>> valueTypes) {
4932         MethodType oldType = target.type();  // get NPE
4933         int dropped = dropArgumentChecks(oldType, pos, valueTypes);
4934         MethodType newType = oldType.insertParameterTypes(pos, valueTypes);
4935         if (dropped == 0)  return target;
4936         BoundMethodHandle result = target.rebind();
4937         LambdaForm lform = result.form;
4938         int insertFormArg = 1 + pos;
4939         for (Class<?> ptype : valueTypes) {
4940             lform = lform.editor().addArgumentForm(insertFormArg++, BasicType.basicType(ptype));
4941         }
4942         result = result.copyWith(newType, lform);
4943         return result;
4944     }
4945 
4946     private static int dropArgumentChecks(MethodType oldType, int pos, List<Class<?>> valueTypes) {
4947         int dropped = valueTypes.size();
4948         MethodType.checkSlotCount(dropped);
4949         int outargs = oldType.parameterCount();
4950         int inargs  = outargs + dropped;
4951         if (pos < 0 || pos > outargs)
4952             throw newIllegalArgumentException("no argument type to remove"
4953                     + Arrays.asList(oldType, pos, valueTypes, inargs, outargs)
4954                     );
4955         return dropped;
4956     }
4957 
4958     /**
4959      * Produces a method handle which will discard some dummy arguments
4960      * before calling some other specified <i>target</i> method handle.
4961      * The type of the new method handle will be the same as the target's type,
4962      * except it will also include the dummy argument types,
4963      * at some given position.
4964      * <p>
4965      * The {@code pos} argument may range between zero and <i>N</i>,
4966      * where <i>N</i> is the arity of the target.
4967      * If {@code pos} is zero, the dummy arguments will precede
4968      * the target's real arguments; if {@code pos} is <i>N</i>
4969      * they will come after.
4970      * @apiNote
4971      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
4972 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodHandles.*;
4973 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodType.*;
4974 ...
4975 MethodHandle cat = lookup().findVirtual(String.class,
4976   "concat", methodType(String.class, String.class));
4977 assertEquals("xy", (String) cat.invokeExact("x", "y"));
4978 MethodHandle d0 = dropArguments(cat, 0, String.class);
4979 assertEquals("yz", (String) d0.invokeExact("x", "y", "z"));
4980 MethodHandle d1 = dropArguments(cat, 1, String.class);
4981 assertEquals("xz", (String) d1.invokeExact("x", "y", "z"));
4982 MethodHandle d2 = dropArguments(cat, 2, String.class);
4983 assertEquals("xy", (String) d2.invokeExact("x", "y", "z"));
4984 MethodHandle d12 = dropArguments(cat, 1, int.class, boolean.class);
4985 assertEquals("xz", (String) d12.invokeExact("x", 12, true, "z"));
4986      * }</pre></blockquote>
4987      * <p>
4988      * This method is also equivalent to the following code:
4989      * <blockquote><pre>
4990      * {@link #dropArguments(MethodHandle,int,List) dropArguments}{@code (target, pos, Arrays.asList(valueTypes))}
4991      * </pre></blockquote>
4992      * @param target the method handle to invoke after the arguments are dropped
4993      * @param pos position of first argument to drop (zero for the leftmost)
4994      * @param valueTypes the type(s) of the argument(s) to drop
4995      * @return a method handle which drops arguments of the given types,
4996      *         before calling the original method handle
4997      * @throws NullPointerException if the target is null,
4998      *                              or if the {@code valueTypes} array or any of its elements is null
4999      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if any element of {@code valueTypes} is {@code void.class},
5000      *                  or if {@code pos} is negative or greater than the arity of the target,
5001      *                  or if the new method handle's type would have
5002      *                  <a href="MethodHandle.html#maxarity">too many parameters</a>
5003      */
5004     public static MethodHandle dropArguments(MethodHandle target, int pos, Class<?>... valueTypes) {
5005         return dropArguments0(target, pos, copyTypes(valueTypes));
5006     }
5007 
5008     // private version which allows caller some freedom with error handling
5009     private static MethodHandle dropArgumentsToMatch(MethodHandle target, int skip, List<Class<?>> newTypes, int pos,
5010                                       boolean nullOnFailure) {
5011         newTypes = copyTypes(newTypes.toArray());
5012         List<Class<?>> oldTypes = target.type().parameterList();
5013         int match = oldTypes.size();
5014         if (skip != 0) {
5015             if (skip < 0 || skip > match) {
5016                 throw newIllegalArgumentException("illegal skip", skip, target);
5017             }
5018             oldTypes = oldTypes.subList(skip, match);
5019             match -= skip;
5020         }
5021         List<Class<?>> addTypes = newTypes;
5022         int add = addTypes.size();
5023         if (pos != 0) {
5024             if (pos < 0 || pos > add) {
5025                 throw newIllegalArgumentException("illegal pos", pos, newTypes);
5026             }
5027             addTypes = addTypes.subList(pos, add);
5028             add -= pos;
5029             assert(addTypes.size() == add);
5030         }
5031         // Do not add types which already match the existing arguments.
5032         if (match > add || !oldTypes.equals(addTypes.subList(0, match))) {
5033             if (nullOnFailure) {
5034                 return null;
5035             }
5036             throw newIllegalArgumentException("argument lists do not match", oldTypes, newTypes);
5037         }
5038         addTypes = addTypes.subList(match, add);
5039         add -= match;
5040         assert(addTypes.size() == add);
5041         // newTypes:     (   P*[pos], M*[match], A*[add] )
5042         // target: ( S*[skip],        M*[match]  )
5043         MethodHandle adapter = target;
5044         if (add > 0) {
5045             adapter = dropArguments0(adapter, skip+ match, addTypes);
5046         }
5047         // adapter: (S*[skip],        M*[match], A*[add] )
5048         if (pos > 0) {
5049             adapter = dropArguments0(adapter, skip, newTypes.subList(0, pos));
5050         }
5051         // adapter: (S*[skip], P*[pos], M*[match], A*[add] )
5052         return adapter;
5053     }
5054 
5055     /**
5056      * Adapts a target method handle to match the given parameter type list. If necessary, adds dummy arguments. Some
5057      * leading parameters can be skipped before matching begins. The remaining types in the {@code target}'s parameter
5058      * type list must be a sub-list of the {@code newTypes} type list at the starting position {@code pos}. The
5059      * resulting handle will have the target handle's parameter type list, with any non-matching parameter types (before
5060      * or after the matching sub-list) inserted in corresponding positions of the target's original parameters, as if by
5061      * {@link #dropArguments(MethodHandle, int, Class[])}.
5062      * <p>
5063      * The resulting handle will have the same return type as the target handle.
5064      * <p>
5065      * In more formal terms, assume these two type lists:<ul>
5066      * <li>The target handle has the parameter type list {@code S..., M...}, with as many types in {@code S} as
5067      * indicated by {@code skip}. The {@code M} types are those that are supposed to match part of the given type list,
5068      * {@code newTypes}.
5069      * <li>The {@code newTypes} list contains types {@code P..., M..., A...}, with as many types in {@code P} as
5070      * indicated by {@code pos}. The {@code M} types are precisely those that the {@code M} types in the target handle's
5071      * parameter type list are supposed to match. The types in {@code A} are additional types found after the matching
5072      * sub-list.
5073      * </ul>
5074      * Given these assumptions, the result of an invocation of {@code dropArgumentsToMatch} will have the parameter type
5075      * list {@code S..., P..., M..., A...}, with the {@code P} and {@code A} types inserted as if by
5076      * {@link #dropArguments(MethodHandle, int, Class[])}.
5077      *
5078      * @apiNote
5079      * Two method handles whose argument lists are "effectively identical" (i.e., identical in a common prefix) may be
5080      * mutually converted to a common type by two calls to {@code dropArgumentsToMatch}, as follows:
5081      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5082 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodHandles.*;
5083 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodType.*;
5084 ...
5085 ...
5086 MethodHandle h0 = constant(boolean.class, true);
5087 MethodHandle h1 = lookup().findVirtual(String.class, "concat", methodType(String.class, String.class));
5088 MethodType bigType = h1.type().insertParameterTypes(1, String.class, int.class);
5089 MethodHandle h2 = dropArguments(h1, 0, bigType.parameterList());
5090 if (h1.type().parameterCount() < h2.type().parameterCount())
5091     h1 = dropArgumentsToMatch(h1, 0, h2.type().parameterList(), 0);  // lengthen h1
5092 else
5093     h2 = dropArgumentsToMatch(h2, 0, h1.type().parameterList(), 0);    // lengthen h2
5094 MethodHandle h3 = guardWithTest(h0, h1, h2);
5095 assertEquals("xy", h3.invoke("x", "y", 1, "a", "b", "c"));
5096      * }</pre></blockquote>
5097      * @param target the method handle to adapt
5098      * @param skip number of targets parameters to disregard (they will be unchanged)
5099      * @param newTypes the list of types to match {@code target}'s parameter type list to
5100      * @param pos place in {@code newTypes} where the non-skipped target parameters must occur
5101      * @return a possibly adapted method handle
5102      * @throws NullPointerException if either argument is null
5103      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if any element of {@code newTypes} is {@code void.class},
5104      *         or if {@code skip} is negative or greater than the arity of the target,
5105      *         or if {@code pos} is negative or greater than the newTypes list size,
5106      *         or if {@code newTypes} does not contain the {@code target}'s non-skipped parameter types at position
5107      *         {@code pos}.
5108      * @since 9
5109      */
5110     public static MethodHandle dropArgumentsToMatch(MethodHandle target, int skip, List<Class<?>> newTypes, int pos) {
5111         Objects.requireNonNull(target);
5112         Objects.requireNonNull(newTypes);
5113         return dropArgumentsToMatch(target, skip, newTypes, pos, false);
5114     }
5115 
5116     /**
5117      * Adapts a target method handle by pre-processing
5118      * one or more of its arguments, each with its own unary filter function,
5119      * and then calling the target with each pre-processed argument
5120      * replaced by the result of its corresponding filter function.
5121      * <p>
5122      * The pre-processing is performed by one or more method handles,
5123      * specified in the elements of the {@code filters} array.
5124      * The first element of the filter array corresponds to the {@code pos}
5125      * argument of the target, and so on in sequence.
5126      * The filter functions are invoked in left to right order.
5127      * <p>
5128      * Null arguments in the array are treated as identity functions,
5129      * and the corresponding arguments left unchanged.
5130      * (If there are no non-null elements in the array, the original target is returned.)
5131      * Each filter is applied to the corresponding argument of the adapter.
5132      * <p>
5133      * If a filter {@code F} applies to the {@code N}th argument of
5134      * the target, then {@code F} must be a method handle which
5135      * takes exactly one argument.  The type of {@code F}'s sole argument
5136      * replaces the corresponding argument type of the target
5137      * in the resulting adapted method handle.
5138      * The return type of {@code F} must be identical to the corresponding
5139      * parameter type of the target.
5140      * <p>
5141      * It is an error if there are elements of {@code filters}
5142      * (null or not)
5143      * which do not correspond to argument positions in the target.
5144      * <p><b>Example:</b>
5145      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5146 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodHandles.*;
5147 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodType.*;
5148 ...
5149 MethodHandle cat = lookup().findVirtual(String.class,
5150   "concat", methodType(String.class, String.class));
5151 MethodHandle upcase = lookup().findVirtual(String.class,
5152   "toUpperCase", methodType(String.class));
5153 assertEquals("xy", (String) cat.invokeExact("x", "y"));
5154 MethodHandle f0 = filterArguments(cat, 0, upcase);
5155 assertEquals("Xy", (String) f0.invokeExact("x", "y")); // Xy
5156 MethodHandle f1 = filterArguments(cat, 1, upcase);
5157 assertEquals("xY", (String) f1.invokeExact("x", "y")); // xY
5158 MethodHandle f2 = filterArguments(cat, 0, upcase, upcase);
5159 assertEquals("XY", (String) f2.invokeExact("x", "y")); // XY
5160      * }</pre></blockquote>
5161      * <p>Here is pseudocode for the resulting adapter. In the code, {@code T}
5162      * denotes the return type of both the {@code target} and resulting adapter.
5163      * {@code P}/{@code p} and {@code B}/{@code b} represent the types and values
5164      * of the parameters and arguments that precede and follow the filter position
5165      * {@code pos}, respectively. {@code A[i]}/{@code a[i]} stand for the types and
5166      * values of the filtered parameters and arguments; they also represent the
5167      * return types of the {@code filter[i]} handles. The latter accept arguments
5168      * {@code v[i]} of type {@code V[i]}, which also appear in the signature of
5169      * the resulting adapter.
5170      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5171      * T target(P... p, A[i]... a[i], B... b);
5172      * A[i] filter[i](V[i]);
5173      * T adapter(P... p, V[i]... v[i], B... b) {
5174      *   return target(p..., filter[i](v[i])..., b...);
5175      * }
5176      * }</pre></blockquote>
5177      * <p>
5178      * <em>Note:</em> The resulting adapter is never a {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector
5179      * variable-arity method handle}, even if the original target method handle was.
5180      *
5181      * @param target the method handle to invoke after arguments are filtered
5182      * @param pos the position of the first argument to filter
5183      * @param filters method handles to call initially on filtered arguments
5184      * @return method handle which incorporates the specified argument filtering logic
5185      * @throws NullPointerException if the target is null
5186      *                              or if the {@code filters} array is null
5187      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if a non-null element of {@code filters}
5188      *          does not match a corresponding argument type of target as described above,
5189      *          or if the {@code pos+filters.length} is greater than {@code target.type().parameterCount()},
5190      *          or if the resulting method handle's type would have
5191      *          <a href="MethodHandle.html#maxarity">too many parameters</a>
5192      */
5193     public static MethodHandle filterArguments(MethodHandle target, int pos, MethodHandle... filters) {
5194         // In method types arguments start at index 0, while the LF
5195         // editor have the MH receiver at position 0 - adjust appropriately.
5196         final int MH_RECEIVER_OFFSET = 1;
5197         filterArgumentsCheckArity(target, pos, filters);
5198         MethodHandle adapter = target;
5199 
5200         // keep track of currently matched filters, as to optimize repeated filters
5201         int index = 0;
5202         int[] positions = new int[filters.length];
5203         MethodHandle filter = null;
5204 
5205         // process filters in reverse order so that the invocation of
5206         // the resulting adapter will invoke the filters in left-to-right order
5207         for (int i = filters.length - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
5208             MethodHandle newFilter = filters[i];
5209             if (newFilter == null) continue;  // ignore null elements of filters
5210 
5211             // flush changes on update
5212             if (filter != newFilter) {
5213                 if (filter != null) {
5214                     if (index > 1) {
5215                         adapter = filterRepeatedArgument(adapter, filter, Arrays.copyOf(positions, index));
5216                     } else {
5217                         adapter = filterArgument(adapter, positions[0] - 1, filter);
5218                     }
5219                 }
5220                 filter = newFilter;
5221                 index = 0;
5222             }
5223 
5224             filterArgumentChecks(target, pos + i, newFilter);
5225             positions[index++] = pos + i + MH_RECEIVER_OFFSET;
5226         }
5227         if (index > 1) {
5228             adapter = filterRepeatedArgument(adapter, filter, Arrays.copyOf(positions, index));
5229         } else if (index == 1) {
5230             adapter = filterArgument(adapter, positions[0] - 1, filter);
5231         }
5232         return adapter;
5233     }
5234 
5235     private static MethodHandle filterRepeatedArgument(MethodHandle adapter, MethodHandle filter, int[] positions) {
5236         MethodType targetType = adapter.type();
5237         MethodType filterType = filter.type();
5238         BoundMethodHandle result = adapter.rebind();
5239         Class<?> newParamType = filterType.parameterType(0);
5240 
5241         Class<?>[] ptypes = targetType.ptypes().clone();
5242         for (int pos : positions) {
5243             ptypes[pos - 1] = newParamType;
5244         }
5245         MethodType newType = MethodType.makeImpl(targetType.rtype(), ptypes, true);
5246 
5247         LambdaForm lform = result.editor().filterRepeatedArgumentForm(BasicType.basicType(newParamType), positions);
5248         return result.copyWithExtendL(newType, lform, filter);
5249     }
5250 
5251     /*non-public*/
5252     static MethodHandle filterArgument(MethodHandle target, int pos, MethodHandle filter) {
5253         filterArgumentChecks(target, pos, filter);
5254         MethodType targetType = target.type();
5255         MethodType filterType = filter.type();
5256         BoundMethodHandle result = target.rebind();
5257         Class<?> newParamType = filterType.parameterType(0);
5258         LambdaForm lform = result.editor().filterArgumentForm(1 + pos, BasicType.basicType(newParamType));
5259         MethodType newType = targetType.changeParameterType(pos, newParamType);
5260         result = result.copyWithExtendL(newType, lform, filter);
5261         return result;
5262     }
5263 
5264     private static void filterArgumentsCheckArity(MethodHandle target, int pos, MethodHandle[] filters) {
5265         MethodType targetType = target.type();
5266         int maxPos = targetType.parameterCount();
5267         if (pos + filters.length > maxPos)
5268             throw newIllegalArgumentException("too many filters");
5269     }
5270 
5271     private static void filterArgumentChecks(MethodHandle target, int pos, MethodHandle filter) throws RuntimeException {
5272         MethodType targetType = target.type();
5273         MethodType filterType = filter.type();
5274         if (filterType.parameterCount() != 1
5275             || filterType.returnType() != targetType.parameterType(pos))
5276             throw newIllegalArgumentException("target and filter types do not match", targetType, filterType);
5277     }
5278 
5279     /**
5280      * Adapts a target method handle by pre-processing
5281      * a sub-sequence of its arguments with a filter (another method handle).
5282      * The pre-processed arguments are replaced by the result (if any) of the
5283      * filter function.
5284      * The target is then called on the modified (usually shortened) argument list.
5285      * <p>
5286      * If the filter returns a value, the target must accept that value as
5287      * its argument in position {@code pos}, preceded and/or followed by
5288      * any arguments not passed to the filter.
5289      * If the filter returns void, the target must accept all arguments
5290      * not passed to the filter.
5291      * No arguments are reordered, and a result returned from the filter
5292      * replaces (in order) the whole subsequence of arguments originally
5293      * passed to the adapter.
5294      * <p>
5295      * The argument types (if any) of the filter
5296      * replace zero or one argument types of the target, at position {@code pos},
5297      * in the resulting adapted method handle.
5298      * The return type of the filter (if any) must be identical to the
5299      * argument type of the target at position {@code pos}, and that target argument
5300      * is supplied by the return value of the filter.
5301      * <p>
5302      * In all cases, {@code pos} must be greater than or equal to zero, and
5303      * {@code pos} must also be less than or equal to the target's arity.
5304      * <p><b>Example:</b>
5305      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5306 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodHandles.*;
5307 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodType.*;
5308 ...
5309 MethodHandle deepToString = publicLookup()
5310   .findStatic(Arrays.class, "deepToString", methodType(String.class, Object[].class));
5311 
5312 MethodHandle ts1 = deepToString.asCollector(String[].class, 1);
5313 assertEquals("[strange]", (String) ts1.invokeExact("strange"));
5314 
5315 MethodHandle ts2 = deepToString.asCollector(String[].class, 2);
5316 assertEquals("[up, down]", (String) ts2.invokeExact("up", "down"));
5317 
5318 MethodHandle ts3 = deepToString.asCollector(String[].class, 3);
5319 MethodHandle ts3_ts2 = collectArguments(ts3, 1, ts2);
5320 assertEquals("[top, [up, down], strange]",
5321              (String) ts3_ts2.invokeExact("top", "up", "down", "strange"));
5322 
5323 MethodHandle ts3_ts2_ts1 = collectArguments(ts3_ts2, 3, ts1);
5324 assertEquals("[top, [up, down], [strange]]",
5325              (String) ts3_ts2_ts1.invokeExact("top", "up", "down", "strange"));
5326 
5327 MethodHandle ts3_ts2_ts3 = collectArguments(ts3_ts2, 1, ts3);
5328 assertEquals("[top, [[up, down, strange], charm], bottom]",
5329              (String) ts3_ts2_ts3.invokeExact("top", "up", "down", "strange", "charm", "bottom"));
5330      * }</pre></blockquote>
5331      * <p>Here is pseudocode for the resulting adapter. In the code, {@code T}
5332      * represents the return type of the {@code target} and resulting adapter.
5333      * {@code V}/{@code v} stand for the return type and value of the
5334      * {@code filter}, which are also found in the signature and arguments of
5335      * the {@code target}, respectively, unless {@code V} is {@code void}.
5336      * {@code A}/{@code a} and {@code C}/{@code c} represent the parameter types
5337      * and values preceding and following the collection position, {@code pos},
5338      * in the {@code target}'s signature. They also turn up in the resulting
5339      * adapter's signature and arguments, where they surround
5340      * {@code B}/{@code b}, which represent the parameter types and arguments
5341      * to the {@code filter} (if any).
5342      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5343      * T target(A...,V,C...);
5344      * V filter(B...);
5345      * T adapter(A... a,B... b,C... c) {
5346      *   V v = filter(b...);
5347      *   return target(a...,v,c...);
5348      * }
5349      * // and if the filter has no arguments:
5350      * T target2(A...,V,C...);
5351      * V filter2();
5352      * T adapter2(A... a,C... c) {
5353      *   V v = filter2();
5354      *   return target2(a...,v,c...);
5355      * }
5356      * // and if the filter has a void return:
5357      * T target3(A...,C...);
5358      * void filter3(B...);
5359      * T adapter3(A... a,B... b,C... c) {
5360      *   filter3(b...);
5361      *   return target3(a...,c...);
5362      * }
5363      * }</pre></blockquote>
5364      * <p>
5365      * A collection adapter {@code collectArguments(mh, 0, coll)} is equivalent to
5366      * one which first "folds" the affected arguments, and then drops them, in separate
5367      * steps as follows:
5368      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5369      * mh = MethodHandles.dropArguments(mh, 1, coll.type().parameterList()); //step 2
5370      * mh = MethodHandles.foldArguments(mh, coll); //step 1
5371      * }</pre></blockquote>
5372      * If the target method handle consumes no arguments besides than the result
5373      * (if any) of the filter {@code coll}, then {@code collectArguments(mh, 0, coll)}
5374      * is equivalent to {@code filterReturnValue(coll, mh)}.
5375      * If the filter method handle {@code coll} consumes one argument and produces
5376      * a non-void result, then {@code collectArguments(mh, N, coll)}
5377      * is equivalent to {@code filterArguments(mh, N, coll)}.
5378      * Other equivalences are possible but would require argument permutation.
5379      * <p>
5380      * <em>Note:</em> The resulting adapter is never a {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector
5381      * variable-arity method handle}, even if the original target method handle was.
5382      *
5383      * @param target the method handle to invoke after filtering the subsequence of arguments
5384      * @param pos the position of the first adapter argument to pass to the filter,
5385      *            and/or the target argument which receives the result of the filter
5386      * @param filter method handle to call on the subsequence of arguments
5387      * @return method handle which incorporates the specified argument subsequence filtering logic
5388      * @throws NullPointerException if either argument is null
5389      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if the return type of {@code filter}
5390      *          is non-void and is not the same as the {@code pos} argument of the target,
5391      *          or if {@code pos} is not between 0 and the target's arity, inclusive,
5392      *          or if the resulting method handle's type would have
5393      *          <a href="MethodHandle.html#maxarity">too many parameters</a>
5394      * @see MethodHandles#foldArguments
5395      * @see MethodHandles#filterArguments
5396      * @see MethodHandles#filterReturnValue
5397      */
5398     public static MethodHandle collectArguments(MethodHandle target, int pos, MethodHandle filter) {
5399         MethodType newType = collectArgumentsChecks(target, pos, filter);
5400         MethodType collectorType = filter.type();
5401         BoundMethodHandle result = target.rebind();
5402         LambdaForm lform;
5403         if (collectorType.returnType().isArray() && filter.intrinsicName() == Intrinsic.NEW_ARRAY) {
5404             lform = result.editor().collectArgumentArrayForm(1 + pos, filter);
5405             if (lform != null) {
5406                 return result.copyWith(newType, lform);
5407             }
5408         }
5409         lform = result.editor().collectArgumentsForm(1 + pos, collectorType.basicType());
5410         return result.copyWithExtendL(newType, lform, filter);
5411     }
5412 
5413     private static MethodType collectArgumentsChecks(MethodHandle target, int pos, MethodHandle filter) throws RuntimeException {
5414         MethodType targetType = target.type();
5415         MethodType filterType = filter.type();
5416         Class<?> rtype = filterType.returnType();
5417         List<Class<?>> filterArgs = filterType.parameterList();
5418         if (rtype == void.class) {
5419             return targetType.insertParameterTypes(pos, filterArgs);
5420         }
5421         if (rtype != targetType.parameterType(pos)) {
5422             throw newIllegalArgumentException("target and filter types do not match", targetType, filterType);
5423         }
5424         return targetType.dropParameterTypes(pos, pos+1).insertParameterTypes(pos, filterArgs);
5425     }
5426 
5427     /**
5428      * Adapts a target method handle by post-processing
5429      * its return value (if any) with a filter (another method handle).
5430      * The result of the filter is returned from the adapter.
5431      * <p>
5432      * If the target returns a value, the filter must accept that value as
5433      * its only argument.
5434      * If the target returns void, the filter must accept no arguments.
5435      * <p>
5436      * The return type of the filter
5437      * replaces the return type of the target
5438      * in the resulting adapted method handle.
5439      * The argument type of the filter (if any) must be identical to the
5440      * return type of the target.
5441      * <p><b>Example:</b>
5442      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5443 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodHandles.*;
5444 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodType.*;
5445 ...
5446 MethodHandle cat = lookup().findVirtual(String.class,
5447   "concat", methodType(String.class, String.class));
5448 MethodHandle length = lookup().findVirtual(String.class,
5449   "length", methodType(int.class));
5450 System.out.println((String) cat.invokeExact("x", "y")); // xy
5451 MethodHandle f0 = filterReturnValue(cat, length);
5452 System.out.println((int) f0.invokeExact("x", "y")); // 2
5453      * }</pre></blockquote>
5454      * <p>Here is pseudocode for the resulting adapter. In the code,
5455      * {@code T}/{@code t} represent the result type and value of the
5456      * {@code target}; {@code V}, the result type of the {@code filter}; and
5457      * {@code A}/{@code a}, the types and values of the parameters and arguments
5458      * of the {@code target} as well as the resulting adapter.
5459      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5460      * T target(A...);
5461      * V filter(T);
5462      * V adapter(A... a) {
5463      *   T t = target(a...);
5464      *   return filter(t);
5465      * }
5466      * // and if the target has a void return:
5467      * void target2(A...);
5468      * V filter2();
5469      * V adapter2(A... a) {
5470      *   target2(a...);
5471      *   return filter2();
5472      * }
5473      * // and if the filter has a void return:
5474      * T target3(A...);
5475      * void filter3(V);
5476      * void adapter3(A... a) {
5477      *   T t = target3(a...);
5478      *   filter3(t);
5479      * }
5480      * }</pre></blockquote>
5481      * <p>
5482      * <em>Note:</em> The resulting adapter is never a {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector
5483      * variable-arity method handle}, even if the original target method handle was.
5484      * @param target the method handle to invoke before filtering the return value
5485      * @param filter method handle to call on the return value
5486      * @return method handle which incorporates the specified return value filtering logic
5487      * @throws NullPointerException if either argument is null
5488      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if the argument list of {@code filter}
5489      *          does not match the return type of target as described above
5490      */
5491     public static MethodHandle filterReturnValue(MethodHandle target, MethodHandle filter) {
5492         MethodType targetType = target.type();
5493         MethodType filterType = filter.type();
5494         filterReturnValueChecks(targetType, filterType);
5495         BoundMethodHandle result = target.rebind();
5496         BasicType rtype = BasicType.basicType(filterType.returnType());
5497         LambdaForm lform = result.editor().filterReturnForm(rtype, false);
5498         MethodType newType = targetType.changeReturnType(filterType.returnType());
5499         result = result.copyWithExtendL(newType, lform, filter);
5500         return result;
5501     }
5502 
5503     private static void filterReturnValueChecks(MethodType targetType, MethodType filterType) throws RuntimeException {
5504         Class<?> rtype = targetType.returnType();
5505         int filterValues = filterType.parameterCount();
5506         if (filterValues == 0
5507                 ? (rtype != void.class)
5508                 : (rtype != filterType.parameterType(0) || filterValues != 1))
5509             throw newIllegalArgumentException("target and filter types do not match", targetType, filterType);
5510     }
5511 
5512     /**
5513      * Adapts a target method handle by pre-processing
5514      * some of its arguments, and then calling the target with
5515      * the result of the pre-processing, inserted into the original
5516      * sequence of arguments.
5517      * <p>
5518      * The pre-processing is performed by {@code combiner}, a second method handle.
5519      * Of the arguments passed to the adapter, the first {@code N} arguments
5520      * are copied to the combiner, which is then called.
5521      * (Here, {@code N} is defined as the parameter count of the combiner.)
5522      * After this, control passes to the target, with any result
5523      * from the combiner inserted before the original {@code N} incoming
5524      * arguments.
5525      * <p>
5526      * If the combiner returns a value, the first parameter type of the target
5527      * must be identical with the return type of the combiner, and the next
5528      * {@code N} parameter types of the target must exactly match the parameters
5529      * of the combiner.
5530      * <p>
5531      * If the combiner has a void return, no result will be inserted,
5532      * and the first {@code N} parameter types of the target
5533      * must exactly match the parameters of the combiner.
5534      * <p>
5535      * The resulting adapter is the same type as the target, except that the
5536      * first parameter type is dropped,
5537      * if it corresponds to the result of the combiner.
5538      * <p>
5539      * (Note that {@link #dropArguments(MethodHandle,int,List) dropArguments} can be used to remove any arguments
5540      * that either the combiner or the target does not wish to receive.
5541      * If some of the incoming arguments are destined only for the combiner,
5542      * consider using {@link MethodHandle#asCollector asCollector} instead, since those
5543      * arguments will not need to be live on the stack on entry to the
5544      * target.)
5545      * <p><b>Example:</b>
5546      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5547 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodHandles.*;
5548 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodType.*;
5549 ...
5550 MethodHandle trace = publicLookup().findVirtual(java.io.PrintStream.class,
5551   "println", methodType(void.class, String.class))
5552     .bindTo(System.out);
5553 MethodHandle cat = lookup().findVirtual(String.class,
5554   "concat", methodType(String.class, String.class));
5555 assertEquals("boojum", (String) cat.invokeExact("boo", "jum"));
5556 MethodHandle catTrace = foldArguments(cat, trace);
5557 // also prints "boo":
5558 assertEquals("boojum", (String) catTrace.invokeExact("boo", "jum"));
5559      * }</pre></blockquote>
5560      * <p>Here is pseudocode for the resulting adapter. In the code, {@code T}
5561      * represents the result type of the {@code target} and resulting adapter.
5562      * {@code V}/{@code v} represent the type and value of the parameter and argument
5563      * of {@code target} that precedes the folding position; {@code V} also is
5564      * the result type of the {@code combiner}. {@code A}/{@code a} denote the
5565      * types and values of the {@code N} parameters and arguments at the folding
5566      * position. {@code B}/{@code b} represent the types and values of the
5567      * {@code target} parameters and arguments that follow the folded parameters
5568      * and arguments.
5569      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5570      * // there are N arguments in A...
5571      * T target(V, A[N]..., B...);
5572      * V combiner(A...);
5573      * T adapter(A... a, B... b) {
5574      *   V v = combiner(a...);
5575      *   return target(v, a..., b...);
5576      * }
5577      * // and if the combiner has a void return:
5578      * T target2(A[N]..., B...);
5579      * void combiner2(A...);
5580      * T adapter2(A... a, B... b) {
5581      *   combiner2(a...);
5582      *   return target2(a..., b...);
5583      * }
5584      * }</pre></blockquote>
5585      * <p>
5586      * <em>Note:</em> The resulting adapter is never a {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector
5587      * variable-arity method handle}, even if the original target method handle was.
5588      * @param target the method handle to invoke after arguments are combined
5589      * @param combiner method handle to call initially on the incoming arguments
5590      * @return method handle which incorporates the specified argument folding logic
5591      * @throws NullPointerException if either argument is null
5592      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if {@code combiner}'s return type
5593      *          is non-void and not the same as the first argument type of
5594      *          the target, or if the initial {@code N} argument types
5595      *          of the target
5596      *          (skipping one matching the {@code combiner}'s return type)
5597      *          are not identical with the argument types of {@code combiner}
5598      */
5599     public static MethodHandle foldArguments(MethodHandle target, MethodHandle combiner) {
5600         return foldArguments(target, 0, combiner);
5601     }
5602 
5603     /**
5604      * Adapts a target method handle by pre-processing some of its arguments, starting at a given position, and then
5605      * calling the target with the result of the pre-processing, inserted into the original sequence of arguments just
5606      * before the folded arguments.
5607      * <p>
5608      * This method is closely related to {@link #foldArguments(MethodHandle, MethodHandle)}, but allows to control the
5609      * position in the parameter list at which folding takes place. The argument controlling this, {@code pos}, is a
5610      * zero-based index. The aforementioned method {@link #foldArguments(MethodHandle, MethodHandle)} assumes position
5611      * 0.
5612      *
5613      * @apiNote Example:
5614      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5615     import static java.lang.invoke.MethodHandles.*;
5616     import static java.lang.invoke.MethodType.*;
5617     ...
5618     MethodHandle trace = publicLookup().findVirtual(java.io.PrintStream.class,
5619     "println", methodType(void.class, String.class))
5620     .bindTo(System.out);
5621     MethodHandle cat = lookup().findVirtual(String.class,
5622     "concat", methodType(String.class, String.class));
5623     assertEquals("boojum", (String) cat.invokeExact("boo", "jum"));
5624     MethodHandle catTrace = foldArguments(cat, 1, trace);
5625     // also prints "jum":
5626     assertEquals("boojum", (String) catTrace.invokeExact("boo", "jum"));
5627      * }</pre></blockquote>
5628      * <p>Here is pseudocode for the resulting adapter. In the code, {@code T}
5629      * represents the result type of the {@code target} and resulting adapter.
5630      * {@code V}/{@code v} represent the type and value of the parameter and argument
5631      * of {@code target} that precedes the folding position; {@code V} also is
5632      * the result type of the {@code combiner}. {@code A}/{@code a} denote the
5633      * types and values of the {@code N} parameters and arguments at the folding
5634      * position. {@code Z}/{@code z} and {@code B}/{@code b} represent the types
5635      * and values of the {@code target} parameters and arguments that precede and
5636      * follow the folded parameters and arguments starting at {@code pos},
5637      * respectively.
5638      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5639      * // there are N arguments in A...
5640      * T target(Z..., V, A[N]..., B...);
5641      * V combiner(A...);
5642      * T adapter(Z... z, A... a, B... b) {
5643      *   V v = combiner(a...);
5644      *   return target(z..., v, a..., b...);
5645      * }
5646      * // and if the combiner has a void return:
5647      * T target2(Z..., A[N]..., B...);
5648      * void combiner2(A...);
5649      * T adapter2(Z... z, A... a, B... b) {
5650      *   combiner2(a...);
5651      *   return target2(z..., a..., b...);
5652      * }
5653      * }</pre></blockquote>
5654      * <p>
5655      * <em>Note:</em> The resulting adapter is never a {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector
5656      * variable-arity method handle}, even if the original target method handle was.
5657      *
5658      * @param target the method handle to invoke after arguments are combined
5659      * @param pos the position at which to start folding and at which to insert the folding result; if this is {@code
5660      *            0}, the effect is the same as for {@link #foldArguments(MethodHandle, MethodHandle)}.
5661      * @param combiner method handle to call initially on the incoming arguments
5662      * @return method handle which incorporates the specified argument folding logic
5663      * @throws NullPointerException if either argument is null
5664      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if either of the following two conditions holds:
5665      *          (1) {@code combiner}'s return type is non-{@code void} and not the same as the argument type at position
5666      *              {@code pos} of the target signature;
5667      *          (2) the {@code N} argument types at position {@code pos} of the target signature (skipping one matching
5668      *              the {@code combiner}'s return type) are not identical with the argument types of {@code combiner}.
5669      *
5670      * @see #foldArguments(MethodHandle, MethodHandle)
5671      * @since 9
5672      */
5673     public static MethodHandle foldArguments(MethodHandle target, int pos, MethodHandle combiner) {
5674         MethodType targetType = target.type();
5675         MethodType combinerType = combiner.type();
5676         Class<?> rtype = foldArgumentChecks(pos, targetType, combinerType);
5677         BoundMethodHandle result = target.rebind();
5678         boolean dropResult = rtype == void.class;
5679         LambdaForm lform = result.editor().foldArgumentsForm(1 + pos, dropResult, combinerType.basicType());
5680         MethodType newType = targetType;
5681         if (!dropResult) {
5682             newType = newType.dropParameterTypes(pos, pos + 1);
5683         }
5684         result = result.copyWithExtendL(newType, lform, combiner);
5685         return result;
5686     }
5687 
5688     private static Class<?> foldArgumentChecks(int foldPos, MethodType targetType, MethodType combinerType) {
5689         int foldArgs   = combinerType.parameterCount();
5690         Class<?> rtype = combinerType.returnType();
5691         int foldVals = rtype == void.class ? 0 : 1;
5692         int afterInsertPos = foldPos + foldVals;
5693         boolean ok = (targetType.parameterCount() >= afterInsertPos + foldArgs);
5694         if (ok) {
5695             for (int i = 0; i < foldArgs; i++) {
5696                 if (combinerType.parameterType(i) != targetType.parameterType(i + afterInsertPos)) {
5697                     ok = false;
5698                     break;
5699                 }
5700             }
5701         }
5702         if (ok && foldVals != 0 && combinerType.returnType() != targetType.parameterType(foldPos))
5703             ok = false;
5704         if (!ok)
5705             throw misMatchedTypes("target and combiner types", targetType, combinerType);
5706         return rtype;
5707     }
5708 
5709     /**
5710      * Adapts a target method handle by pre-processing some of its arguments, then calling the target with the result
5711      * of the pre-processing replacing the argument at the given position.
5712      *
5713      * @param target the method handle to invoke after arguments are combined
5714      * @param position the position at which to start folding and at which to insert the folding result; if this is {@code
5715      *            0}, the effect is the same as for {@link #foldArguments(MethodHandle, MethodHandle)}.
5716      * @param combiner method handle to call initially on the incoming arguments
5717      * @param argPositions indexes of the target to pick arguments sent to the combiner from
5718      * @return method handle which incorporates the specified argument folding logic
5719      * @throws NullPointerException if either argument is null
5720      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if either of the following two conditions holds:
5721      *          (1) {@code combiner}'s return type is not the same as the argument type at position
5722      *              {@code pos} of the target signature;
5723      *          (2) the {@code N} argument types at positions {@code argPositions[1...N]} of the target signature are
5724      *              not identical with the argument types of {@code combiner}.
5725      */
5726     /*non-public*/
5727     static MethodHandle filterArgumentsWithCombiner(MethodHandle target, int position, MethodHandle combiner, int ... argPositions) {
5728         return argumentsWithCombiner(true, target, position, combiner, argPositions);
5729     }
5730 
5731     /**
5732      * Adapts a target method handle by pre-processing some of its arguments, calling the target with the result of
5733      * the pre-processing inserted into the original sequence of arguments at the given position.
5734      *
5735      * @param target the method handle to invoke after arguments are combined
5736      * @param position the position at which to start folding and at which to insert the folding result; if this is {@code
5737      *            0}, the effect is the same as for {@link #foldArguments(MethodHandle, MethodHandle)}.
5738      * @param combiner method handle to call initially on the incoming arguments
5739      * @param argPositions indexes of the target to pick arguments sent to the combiner from
5740      * @return method handle which incorporates the specified argument folding logic
5741      * @throws NullPointerException if either argument is null
5742      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if either of the following two conditions holds:
5743      *          (1) {@code combiner}'s return type is non-{@code void} and not the same as the argument type at position
5744      *              {@code pos} of the target signature;
5745      *          (2) the {@code N} argument types at positions {@code argPositions[1...N]} of the target signature
5746      *              (skipping {@code position} where the {@code combiner}'s return will be folded in) are not identical
5747      *              with the argument types of {@code combiner}.
5748      */
5749     /*non-public*/
5750     static MethodHandle foldArgumentsWithCombiner(MethodHandle target, int position, MethodHandle combiner, int ... argPositions) {
5751         return argumentsWithCombiner(false, target, position, combiner, argPositions);
5752     }
5753 
5754     private static MethodHandle argumentsWithCombiner(boolean filter, MethodHandle target, int position, MethodHandle combiner, int ... argPositions) {
5755         MethodType targetType = target.type();
5756         MethodType combinerType = combiner.type();
5757         Class<?> rtype = argumentsWithCombinerChecks(position, filter, targetType, combinerType, argPositions);
5758         BoundMethodHandle result = target.rebind();
5759 
5760         MethodType newType = targetType;
5761         LambdaForm lform;
5762         if (filter) {
5763             lform = result.editor().filterArgumentsForm(1 + position, combinerType.basicType(), argPositions);
5764         } else {
5765             boolean dropResult = rtype == void.class;
5766             lform = result.editor().foldArgumentsForm(1 + position, dropResult, combinerType.basicType(), argPositions);
5767             if (!dropResult) {
5768                 newType = newType.dropParameterTypes(position, position + 1);
5769             }
5770         }
5771         result = result.copyWithExtendL(newType, lform, combiner);
5772         return result;
5773     }
5774 
5775     private static Class<?> argumentsWithCombinerChecks(int position, boolean filter, MethodType targetType, MethodType combinerType, int ... argPos) {
5776         int combinerArgs = combinerType.parameterCount();
5777         if (argPos.length != combinerArgs) {
5778             throw newIllegalArgumentException("combiner and argument map must be equal size", combinerType, argPos.length);
5779         }
5780         Class<?> rtype = combinerType.returnType();
5781 
5782         for (int i = 0; i < combinerArgs; i++) {
5783             int arg = argPos[i];
5784             if (arg < 0 || arg > targetType.parameterCount()) {
5785                 throw newIllegalArgumentException("arg outside of target parameterRange", targetType, arg);
5786             }
5787             if (combinerType.parameterType(i) != targetType.parameterType(arg)) {
5788                 throw newIllegalArgumentException("target argument type at position " + arg
5789                         + " must match combiner argument type at index " + i + ": " + targetType
5790                         + " -> " + combinerType + ", map: " + Arrays.toString(argPos));
5791             }
5792         }
5793         if (filter && combinerType.returnType() != targetType.parameterType(position)) {
5794             throw misMatchedTypes("target and combiner types", targetType, combinerType);
5795         }
5796         return rtype;
5797     }
5798 
5799     /**
5800      * Makes a method handle which adapts a target method handle,
5801      * by guarding it with a test, a boolean-valued method handle.
5802      * If the guard fails, a fallback handle is called instead.
5803      * All three method handles must have the same corresponding
5804      * argument and return types, except that the return type
5805      * of the test must be boolean, and the test is allowed
5806      * to have fewer arguments than the other two method handles.
5807      * <p>
5808      * Here is pseudocode for the resulting adapter. In the code, {@code T}
5809      * represents the uniform result type of the three involved handles;
5810      * {@code A}/{@code a}, the types and values of the {@code target}
5811      * parameters and arguments that are consumed by the {@code test}; and
5812      * {@code B}/{@code b}, those types and values of the {@code target}
5813      * parameters and arguments that are not consumed by the {@code test}.
5814      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5815      * boolean test(A...);
5816      * T target(A...,B...);
5817      * T fallback(A...,B...);
5818      * T adapter(A... a,B... b) {
5819      *   if (test(a...))
5820      *     return target(a..., b...);
5821      *   else
5822      *     return fallback(a..., b...);
5823      * }
5824      * }</pre></blockquote>
5825      * Note that the test arguments ({@code a...} in the pseudocode) cannot
5826      * be modified by execution of the test, and so are passed unchanged
5827      * from the caller to the target or fallback as appropriate.
5828      * @param test method handle used for test, must return boolean
5829      * @param target method handle to call if test passes
5830      * @param fallback method handle to call if test fails
5831      * @return method handle which incorporates the specified if/then/else logic
5832      * @throws NullPointerException if any argument is null
5833      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if {@code test} does not return boolean,
5834      *          or if all three method types do not match (with the return
5835      *          type of {@code test} changed to match that of the target).
5836      */
5837     public static MethodHandle guardWithTest(MethodHandle test,
5838                                MethodHandle target,
5839                                MethodHandle fallback) {
5840         MethodType gtype = test.type();
5841         MethodType ttype = target.type();
5842         MethodType ftype = fallback.type();
5843         if (!ttype.equals(ftype))
5844             throw misMatchedTypes("target and fallback types", ttype, ftype);
5845         if (gtype.returnType() != boolean.class)
5846             throw newIllegalArgumentException("guard type is not a predicate "+gtype);
5847         List<Class<?>> targs = ttype.parameterList();
5848         test = dropArgumentsToMatch(test, 0, targs, 0, true);
5849         if (test == null) {
5850             throw misMatchedTypes("target and test types", ttype, gtype);
5851         }
5852         return MethodHandleImpl.makeGuardWithTest(test, target, fallback);
5853     }
5854 
5855     static <T> RuntimeException misMatchedTypes(String what, T t1, T t2) {
5856         return newIllegalArgumentException(what + " must match: " + t1 + " != " + t2);
5857     }
5858 
5859     /**
5860      * Makes a method handle which adapts a target method handle,
5861      * by running it inside an exception handler.
5862      * If the target returns normally, the adapter returns that value.
5863      * If an exception matching the specified type is thrown, the fallback
5864      * handle is called instead on the exception, plus the original arguments.
5865      * <p>
5866      * The target and handler must have the same corresponding
5867      * argument and return types, except that handler may omit trailing arguments
5868      * (similarly to the predicate in {@link #guardWithTest guardWithTest}).
5869      * Also, the handler must have an extra leading parameter of {@code exType} or a supertype.
5870      * <p>
5871      * Here is pseudocode for the resulting adapter. In the code, {@code T}
5872      * represents the return type of the {@code target} and {@code handler},
5873      * and correspondingly that of the resulting adapter; {@code A}/{@code a},
5874      * the types and values of arguments to the resulting handle consumed by
5875      * {@code handler}; and {@code B}/{@code b}, those of arguments to the
5876      * resulting handle discarded by {@code handler}.
5877      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5878      * T target(A..., B...);
5879      * T handler(ExType, A...);
5880      * T adapter(A... a, B... b) {
5881      *   try {
5882      *     return target(a..., b...);
5883      *   } catch (ExType ex) {
5884      *     return handler(ex, a...);
5885      *   }
5886      * }
5887      * }</pre></blockquote>
5888      * Note that the saved arguments ({@code a...} in the pseudocode) cannot
5889      * be modified by execution of the target, and so are passed unchanged
5890      * from the caller to the handler, if the handler is invoked.
5891      * <p>
5892      * The target and handler must return the same type, even if the handler
5893      * always throws.  (This might happen, for instance, because the handler
5894      * is simulating a {@code finally} clause).
5895      * To create such a throwing handler, compose the handler creation logic
5896      * with {@link #throwException throwException},
5897      * in order to create a method handle of the correct return type.
5898      * @param target method handle to call
5899      * @param exType the type of exception which the handler will catch
5900      * @param handler method handle to call if a matching exception is thrown
5901      * @return method handle which incorporates the specified try/catch logic
5902      * @throws NullPointerException if any argument is null
5903      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if {@code handler} does not accept
5904      *          the given exception type, or if the method handle types do
5905      *          not match in their return types and their
5906      *          corresponding parameters
5907      * @see MethodHandles#tryFinally(MethodHandle, MethodHandle)
5908      */
5909     public static MethodHandle catchException(MethodHandle target,
5910                                 Class<? extends Throwable> exType,
5911                                 MethodHandle handler) {
5912         MethodType ttype = target.type();
5913         MethodType htype = handler.type();
5914         if (!Throwable.class.isAssignableFrom(exType))
5915             throw new ClassCastException(exType.getName());
5916         if (htype.parameterCount() < 1 ||
5917             !htype.parameterType(0).isAssignableFrom(exType))
